ุชุญูู ฺฉู:
ุจุฑุง ุชุนูู ุงู ุชุญูู ุจู ฺฉู ุฏุงุฏูโูุงุ ุจุงุฏ ุจุฑุง ุชูุงู ุจุงุฒูโูุง ต ุฏูููโุง ุงูุฌุงู ุดูุฏ. ุจุง ุชูุฌู ุจู ุญุฌู ุฏุงุฏูโูุงุ ูพุดููุงุฏ ูโุดูุฏ ุงุฒ ฺฉ ุงุณฺฉุฑูพุช ุจุฑูุงููโููุณ (ูุซูุงู Python ุจุง ฺฉุชุงุจุฎุงูู Pandas) ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ุดูุฏ:

ุจุฑุง ูุฑ ฺฉูุฏู ุจุฑุฑุณ ุดูุฏ ฺฉู ุขุง Open_t > Open_t-1 ุงุณุช.

ุฏุฑุตุฏ ุงูุฒุงุด ุฏุฑ ุญุงูุช Open_t > Open_t-1 ูุญุงุณุจู ุดูุฏ.
ููููู ฺฉุฏ ูพุงุชูู ุจุฑุง ุชุญูู:

import pandas as pd

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])

# ุชุจุฏู ุฒูุงู ุจู ูุฑูุช datetime
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')

# ุชูุธู ุชุงูโูุฑู ต ุฏูููโุง
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last'}).dropna()

# ูุญุงุณุจู Open_t > Open_t-1
data_5min['Open_Higher'] = data_5min['Open'] > data_5min['Open'].shift(1)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close'] > data_5min['Close'].shift(1)

# ุชุญูู ุชุฃุซุฑ
result = data_5min.groupby('Open_Higher')['Trend_Up'].mean()
print("ุงุญุชูุงู ุฑููุฏ ุตุนูุฏ ููุช Open_t > Open_t-1:", result[True])
print("ุงุญุชูุงู ุฑููุฏ ุตุนูุฏ ููุช Open_t <= Open_t-1:", result[False])

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)

# ุชุจุฏู ุจู ุชุงูโูุฑู ต ุฏูููโุง
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last'}).dropna()

# ูุญุงุณุจู ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Open_Higher'] = data_5min['Open_Diff'] > 0
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0

# ุชุญูู ุชุฃุซุฑ Open_Higher ุจุฑ ุฑููุฏ
trend_analysis = data_5min.groupby('Open_Higher')['Trend_Up'].mean()
print("ุงุญุชูุงู ุฑููุฏ ุตุนูุฏ:")
print(f"ููุช Open_t > Open_t-1: {trend_analysis[True]:.2%}")
print(f"ููุช Open_t <= Open_t-1: {trend_analysis[False]:.2%}")

# ุฑุณู ูููุฏุงุฑ ููุช
plt.figure(figsize=(12, 6))
plt.plot(data_5min.index, data_5min['Close'], label='Close Price')
plt.title('XAUUSD 5-Minute Close Price')
plt.xlabel('Time')
plt.ylabel('Price')
plt.legend()
plt.show()

def is_bullish_engulfing(df):
    return (df['Close'].shift(1) < df['Open'].shift(1)) & \
           (df['Close'] > df['Open']) & \
           (df['Close'] > df['Open'].shift(1)) & \
           (df['Open'] < df['Close'].shift(1))

ูุฏู ุทุฑุงุญ ูุงุดู :
ฺฉ ูุฏู ุฌูฺฏู ุชุตุงุฏู (Random Forest) ุจุฑุง ูพุดโุจู ุฑููุฏ ูพุดุฑูุช/ูุฒูู ูพุงุฏูโุณุงุฒ ูโฺฉูู.
ูฺฺฏ ูุง: Open_Diff ุ Range ุ RSI ุ MACD ุ ุณุงุนุช ุฑูุฒ.
ูุฏู: ูพุดโุจู Trend_Up = (Close_t > Close_t-1) .
ุจุตุฑ ุณุงุฒ :
ูููุฏุงุฑูุง ููุชุ ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑูุงุ ู ุฎูุดูโูุง ุฑุง ุจุง Plotly ุฑุณู ูโฺฉูู.
ุฏุงุดุจูุฑุฏ ุดุฑฺฉุช ูโุณุงุฒู ฺฉู ุงูฺฏููุง ู ูุดุงููโูุง ุฑุง ูุดุงู ูโุฏูุฏ.
ฺฉุฏ ููููู ูพุดุฑูุชู :

ูพุงุชูู
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)

# ุชุจุฏู ุจู ุชุงูโูุฑู ต ุฏูููโุง
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last'}).dropna()

# ูุญุงุณุจู ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0

# ุญุฐู ููุงุฏุฑ NaN
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# ูุฏู ุฌูฺฏู ุชุตุงุฏู
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'Hour']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.3, random_state=42)

model = RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=100, random_state=42)
model.fit(X_train, y_train)
y_pred = model.predict(X_test)
print(f"ุฏูุช ูุฏู: {accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred):.2%}")

# ุงููุช ูฺฺฏโูุง
feature_importance = pd.Series(model.feature_importances_, index=features)
print("ุงููุช ูฺฺฏโูุง:\n", feature_importance)

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ ููุช ู ุณฺฏูุงูโูุง
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.update_layout(title='XAUUSD 5-Minute Candlestick Chart', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()

def is_bullish_engulfing(df):
    return (df['Close'].shift(1) < df['Open'].shift(1)) & \
           (df['Close'] > df['Open']) & \
           (df['Close'] > df['Open'].shift(1)) & \
           (df['Open'] < df['Close'].shift(1))

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
from sklearn.cluster import DBSCAN
from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential
from tensorflow.keras.layers import LSTM, Dense
from sklearn.preprocessing import MinMaxScaler
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)

# ุชุจุฏู ุจู ุชุงูโูุฑู ต ุฏูููโุง
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last'}).dropna()

# ูุญุงุณุจู ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0

# ุญุฐู NaN
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# ูุฏู ุฌูฺฏู ุชุตุงุฏู
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Hour']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.3, random_state=42)
rf_model = RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=100, random_state=42)
rf_model.fit(X_train, y_train)
y_pred = rf_model.predict(X_test)
print(f"ุฏูุช ุฌูฺฏู ุชุตุงุฏู: {accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred):.2%}")

# ุฎูุดูโุจูุฏ ุจุง DBSCAN
clustering_features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'Close_Diff']
scaler = MinMaxScaler()
X_cluster = scaler.fit_transform(data_5min[clustering_features].dropna())
dbscan = DBSCAN(eps=0.3, min_samples=5)
data_5min['Cluster'] = dbscan.fit_predict(X_cluster)
outliers = data_5min[data_5min['Cluster'] == -1]
print(f"ุชุนุฏุงุฏ ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ (Outliers): {len(outliers)}")

# ูุฏู LSTM
scaler = MinMaxScaler()
scaled_data = scaler.fit_transform(data_5min[['Close']].values)
X_lstm, y_lstm = [], []
for i in range(60, len(scaled_data)):
    X_lstm.append(scaled_data[i-60:i])
    y_lstm.append(scaled_data[i])
X_lstm, y_lstm = np.array(X_lstm), np.array(y_lstm)
X_train_lstm, X_test_lstm, y_train_lstm, y_test_lstm = train_test_split(X_lstm, y_lstm, test_size=0.3, random_state=42)

lstm_model = Sequential()
lstm_model.add(LSTM(50, return_sequences=True, input_shape=(X_lstm.shape[1], 1)))
lstm_model.add(LSTM(50))
lstm_model.add(Dense(1))
lstm_model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='mse')
lstm_model.fit(X_train_lstm, y_train_lstm, epochs=10, batch_size=32, verbose=0)
lstm_predictions = lstm_model.predict(X_test_lstm)
print("ูุฏู LSTM ุขููุฒุด ุฏุงุฏู ุดุฏ.")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=outliers.index, y=outliers['Close'], mode='markers', name='Outliers', marker=dict(color='red', size=10)))
fig.update_layout(title='XAUUSD 5-Minute Chart with Outliers', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()

def is_multi_candle_pattern(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    large_range = (df['Range'] > 2 * df['ATR'])
    return doji & open_higher & large_range
ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑูุง ู ุดุงุฎุต ุชุฑฺฉุจ :
ุจุง TA-Libุ ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑูุง RSIุ MACDุ ATRุ ู Stochastic ุฑุง ูุญุงุณุจู ูโฺฉูู.
ุดุงุฎุต ุชุฑฺฉุจ ุฑุง ุจุง ุงูฺฏูุฑุชู ฺูุชฺฉ ุจูููโุณุงุฒ ูโฺฉูู.

ูุงููู ฺฉูุฏู ุจุง ูุธุฑูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ.

ุชุฎูู ุงุญุชูุงู ูพุดโุจูโูุง (ุงุฒ ูุฏู ุจุฒ).

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential
from tensorflow.keras.layers import LSTM, Dense, Dropout
from tensorflow.keras.layers import Dense
from sklearn.preprocessing import MinMaxScaler
import networkx as nx
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from deap import base, creator, tools, algorithms
import random

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)

# ุชุจุฏู ุจู ุชุงูโูุฑู ต ุฏูููโุง
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last'}).dropna()

# ูุญุงุณุจู ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Stochastic'], _ = talib.STOCH(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0

# ุญุฐู NaN
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# ุจูููโุณุงุฒ ุดุงุฎุต ุชุฑฺฉุจ ุจุง ุงูฺฏูุฑุชู ฺูุชฺฉ
def composite_signal(weights, data):
    rsi_score = (data['RSI'] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data['MACD'] - data['MACD_Signal']) / data['ATR']
    atr_score = data['ATR'] / data['ATR'].mean()
    signal = weights[0] * rsi_score + weights[1] * macd_score + weights[2] * atr_score
    return signal

creator.create("FitnessMax", base.Fitness, weights=(1.0,))
creator.create("Individual", list, fitness=creator.FitnessMax)

toolbox = base.Toolbox()
toolbox.register("attr_float", random.uniform, 0, 1)
toolbox.register("individual", tools.initRepeat, creator.Individual, toolbox.attr_float, n=3)
toolbox.register("population", tools.initRepeat, list, toolbox.individual)

def evaluate(individual):
    data_5min['Composite_Signal'] = composite_signal(individual, data_5min)
    signals = (data_5min['Composite_Signal'] > 0) & (data_5min['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    returns = data_5min[signals]['Close_Diff'].sum()
    return returns,

toolbox.register("evaluate", evaluate)
toolbox.register("mate", tools.cxBlend, alpha=0.5)
toolbox.register("mutate", tools.mutGaussian, mu=0, sigma=0.1, indpb=0.2)
toolbox.register("select", tools.selTournament, tournsize=3)

population = toolbox.population(n=50)
algorithms.eaSimple(population, toolbox, cxpb=0.5, mutpb=0.2, ngen=40, verbose=False)
best_weights = tools.selBest(population, k=1)[0]
print(f"ูุฒูโูุง ุจููู ุดุงุฎุต ุชุฑฺฉุจ: {best_weights}")

# ูุฏู ุฌูฺฏู ุชุตุงุฏู
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Stochastic', 'Hour', 'Composite_Signal']
data_5min['Composite_Signal'] = composite_signal(best_weights, data_5min)
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.3, random_state=42)
rf_model = RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=100, random_state=42)
rf_model.fit(X_train, y_train)
y_pred = rf_model.predict(X_test)
print(f"ุฏูุช ุฌูฺฏู ุชุตุงุฏู: {accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred):.2%}")

# ุชุญูู ุดุจฺฉู
G = nx.Graph()
for i in range(len(data_5min) - 1):
    for j in range(i + 1, len(data_5min)):
        similarity = 1 / (1 + abs(data_5min['Range'].iloc[i] - data_5min['Range'].iloc[j]))
        if similarity > 0.9:
            G.add_edge(i, j, weight=similarity)
central_nodes = sorted(nx.degree_centrality(G).items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:10]
central_indices = [node[0] for node in central_nodes]
print(f"ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ูุฑฺฉุฒ ุฏุฑ ุดุจฺฉู: {central_indices}")

# Autoencoder ุจุฑุง ุดูุงุณุง ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ
scaler = MinMaxScaler()
X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(data_5min[['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'Close_Diff']].dropna())
autoencoder = Sequential([
    Dense(16, activation='relu', input_shape=(X_scaled.shape[1],)),
    Dense(8, activation='relu'),
    Dense(16, activation='relu'),
    Dense(X_scaled.shape[1], activation='linear')
])
autoencoder.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='mse')
autoencoder.fit(X_scaled, X_scaled, epochs=50, batch_size=32, verbose=0)
reconstructions = autoencoder.predict(X_scaled)
mse = np.mean(np.power(X_scaled - reconstructions, 2), axis=1)
outliers = data_5min.iloc[np.where(mse > np.percentile(mse, 95))[0]]
print(f"ุชุนุฏุงุฏ ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ (Autoencoder): {len(outliers)}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=outliers.index, y=outliers['Close'], mode='markers', name='Outliers', marker=dict(color='red', size=10)))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index[central_indices], y=data_5min['Close'].iloc[central_indices], mode='markers', name='Central Nodes', marker=dict(color='blue', size=12)))
fig.update_layout(title='XAUUSD 5-Minute Chart with Outliers and Central Nodes', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()
ูุฑุญูู ด: ฺฉุงูุด ุฎูุงูุงูู - ุงููุงู ุงุฒ ุนููู ุฏฺฏุฑ
ุจุฑุง ฺฉุดู ุฑุงุฒ ูููุชูุ ุจุงุฏ ุงุฒ ุนููู ุฏฺฏุฑ ุงููุงู ุจฺฏุฑู ู ุงุฏูโูุง ูุชุนุงุฑู ุฑุง ุขุฒูุงุด ฺฉูู:

ุงููุงู ุงุฒ ุฒุณุชโุดูุงุณ - ุฑูุชุงุฑ ุฌูุน :
ูุฑุถ ูโฺฉูู ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ (Outliers) ูุงููุฏ ุฑูุชุงุฑูุง ุฌูุน ุฏุฑ ุทุจุนุช (ูุซู ุญุฑฺฉุช ฺฏููโูุง) ูุณุชูุฏ. ุขุง ุงู ุชูุงูู ุจูโุตูุฑุช ููุงููฺฏ ูุจู ุงุฒ ุชุบุฑ ููุชโูุง ุจุฒุฑฺฏ ุธุงูุฑ ูโุดูุฏุ

          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal'])) & \
          (data_5min['Hour'].isin([8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16])) & \

ูุซูุงู:
ูพุงุชูู
def multi_candle_pattern_score(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    breakout = (df['Close'] > df['High'].shift(1).rolling(50).max())
    score = 0.4 * doji.astype(int) + 0.3 * open_higher.astype(int) + 0.3 * breakout.astype(int)
    return score

ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑูุง RSIุ MACDุ ATRุ Stochasticุ Ichimokuุ ู ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑ ุทุจู.

ูพุงุชูู
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from sklearn.ensemble import GradientBoostingClassifier
from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential
from tensorflow.keras.layers import LSTM, Dense, Dropout
from tensorflow.keras.layers import Dense, Input
from sklearn.preprocessing import MinMaxScaler
import networkx as nx
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from pykalman import KalmanFilter
from deap import base, creator, tools, algorithms
import random
from scipy import signal

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)

# ุชุจุฏู ุจู ุชุงูโูุฑู ต ุฏูููโุง
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last'}).dropna()

# ูุญุงุณุจู ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Stochastic'], _ = talib.STOCH(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['Ichimoku_Tenkan'], _, _, _, _ = talib.ICHIMOKU(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['Pattern_Score'] = multi_candle_pattern_score(data_5min)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0

# ุญุฐู NaN
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑ ุชุทุจู ุจุง Kalman Filter
kf = KalmanFilter(initial_state_mean=0, n_dim_obs=1)
data_5min['Adaptive_Signal'] = 0.0
for i in range(1, len(data_5min)):
    rsi_score = (data_5min['RSI'].iloc[i] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data_5min['MACD'].iloc[i] - data_5min['MACD_Signal'].iloc[i]) / data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i]
    atr_score = data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i] / data_5min['ATR'].mean()
    observation = np.array([[0.4 * rsi_score + 0.3 * macd_score + 0.3 * atr_score]])
    state, _ = kf.filter_update(kf.initial_state_mean, kf.initial_state_covariance, observation)
    data_5min['Adaptive_Signal'].iloc[i] = state[0]

# ุจูููโุณุงุฒ Pattern_Score ุจุง Gradient Boosting
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Stochastic', 'Ichimoku_Tenkan', 'Adaptive_Signal']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.3, random_state=42)
gb_model = GradientBoostingClassifier(n_estimators=100, random_state=42)
gb_model.fit(X_train, y_train)
y_pred = gb_model.predict(X_test)
print(f"ุฏูุช Gradient Boosting: {accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred):.2%}")

# ุชุญูู ุดุจฺฉู ูพูุง
G = nx.Graph()
for t in range(0, len(data_5min) - 50, 50):
    window = data_5min.iloc[t:t+50]
    for i in range(len(window) - 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, len(window)):
            similarity = 1 / (1 + abs(window['Range'].iloc[i] - window['Range'].iloc[j]))
            if similarity > 0.9:
                G.add_edge(t + i, t + j, weight=similarity)
central_nodes = sorted(nx.degree_centrality(G).items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:10]
central_indices = [node[0] for node in central_nodes]
print(f"ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ูุฑฺฉุฒ ุฏุฑ ุดุจฺฉู: {central_indices}")

# Variational Autoencoder
from tensorflow.keras.layers import Lambda
from tensorflow.keras import backend as K

def sampling(args):
    z_mean, z_log_var = args
    epsilon = K.random_normal(shape=(K.shape(z_mean)[0], 8))
    return z_mean + K.exp(0.5 * z_log_var) * epsilon

scaler = MinMaxScaler()
X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(data_5min[['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'Close_Diff']].dropna())
input_dim = X_scaled.shape[1]
vae_input = Input(shape=(input_dim,))
h = Dense(16, activation='relu')(vae_input)
z_mean = Dense(8)(h)
z_log_var = Dense(8)(h)
z = Lambda(sampling)([z_mean, z_log_var])
decoder_h = Dense(16, activation='relu')(z)
vae_output = Dense(input_dim)(decoder_h)
vae = Model(vae_input, vae_output)
vae.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='mse')
vae.fit(X_scaled, X_scaled, epochs=50, batch_size=32, verbose=0)
reconstructions = vae.predict(X_scaled)
mse = np.mean(np.power(X_scaled - reconstructions, 2), axis=1)
outliers = data_5min.iloc[np.where(mse > np.percentile(mse, 95))[0]]
print(f"ุชุนุฏุงุฏ ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ (VAE): {len(outliers)}")

# ุชุญูู ููุฌฺฉ
import pywt
coeffs = pywt.wavedec(data_5min['Close_Diff'].dropna(), 'db1', level=4)
wavelet_freqs = [f"Level {i}" for i in range(len(coeffs))]
print(f"ฺุฑุฎูโูุง ุฒูุงู ุดูุงุณุงโุดุฏู ุชูุณุท ููุฌฺฉ: {wavelet_freqs}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))

fig.update_layout(title='XAUUSD 5-Minute Chart with Outliers, Central Nodes, and Adaptive Signal', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()

ูุฑุญูู 5: ุณุณุชู ุณุณุชู ุฎูุฏฺฉุงุฑ ู ุจฺฉโุชุณุช

          (data_5min['Adaptive_Signal'] > 0) & \
          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal'])) & \
          (data_5min['Hour'].isin([8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16])) & \
          (~data_5min.index.isin(outliers.index)) & (~data_5min.index.isin(data_5min.index[central_indices]))
data_5min['Signal'] = signals
data_5min['Returns'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'].shift(-1)

ุฏุงุฏูโูุง ุฑุง ุจู ุชุงูโูุฑูโูุง ตุ ฑตุ ถฐ ุฏูููุ ุฑูุฒุงููุ ู ููุชฺฏ ูโฺฉูู.
ุณุชููโูุง ุฌุฏุฏ: Open_Diff ุ Close_Diff ุ Range ุ RSIุ MACDุ ATRุ Stochasticุ Ichimokuุ Bollinger Bandsุ Cosmic_Signalุ Cosmic_Pattern_Scoreุ ู ุดุงุฎุตโูุง ุดุจฺฉูโูุง.
ุงูฺฏููุง ฺฉูุงู :
ุงูฺฏูุฑุชู ุจุฑุง ุดูุงุณุง ุงูฺฏููุง ฺูุฏ ฺฉูุฏู ุจุง ุงูุชุงุฒุฏู ฺฉูุงู ุทุฑุงุญ ูโฺฉูู:
ูพุงุชูู
def cosmic_pattern_score(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    breakout = (df['Close'] > df['High'].shift(1).rolling(50).max())
    volume_surge = (df['Volume'] > df['Volume'].rolling(20).mean() * 1.5).shift(1)
    score = 0.3 * doji.astype(int) + 0.3 * open_higher.astype(int) + 0.2 * breakout.astype(int) + 0.2 * volume_surge.astype(int)
    return score
ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑ ุทุจู โโฺฉูุงู :
Cosmic_Signal ุฑุง ุจุง Extended Kalman Filter ูพุงุฏูโุณุงุฒ ูโฺฉูู.
ูุฒูโูุง ุฑุง ุจุง ฺฉ ูุฏู ุชููุช (Reinforcement Learning) ุจููู ูโฺฉูู.
ููุด ูุตููุน ฺฉูุงู :
XGBoost ู LightGBM : ุจุฑุง ูพุดโุจู Trend_Up ุจุง ุจูููโุณุงุฒ ุจุฒ.
Transformer ู LSTM : ุจุฑุง ูพุดโุจู ุณุฑโูุง ุฒูุงู ุจุง ูุนูุงุฑ ฺูุฏูุงู.
Variational Autoencoder ู Graph Autoencoder : ุจุฑุง ุฎูุดูโุจูุฏ ู ุดูุงุณุง ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ.
GANูุง ูพุดุฑูุชู : ุจุฑุง ุชููุฏ ุฏุงุฏูโูุง ููุช ูุตููุน ู ุดุจูโุณุงุฒ ุณูุงุฑููุง ุจุงุฒุงุฑ.
ุชููุช (Deep Q-Learning) : ุจุฑุง ูุฑูุฏ/ุฎุฑูุฌ ุจููู ุณุงุฒ.
AI ูพุฐุฑูพุฐุฑ (SHAP) : ุจุฑุง ุงุฑุงุฆู ุฑุงูููุง ุจุฑุง ูุฑ ุชูุถุญ.
ุชุญูู ุดุจฺฉู ูพูุง :
ุจุง Temporal Graph Neural Networksุ ุดุจฺฉูโูุง ูพูุง ุงุฒ ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ูโุณุงุฒูุฏ ู ฺฏุฑูโูุง ูุฑฺฉุฒ ุฑุง ุฏุฑ ูุฑ ุจุงุฒู ุฒูุงู ุดูุงุณุง ูโฺฉููุฏ.
ุจุตุฑ ุณุงุฒ ฺูุฏุฌูุงู :
ุฏุงุดุจูุฑุฏ ฺฉูุงู ุจุง Plotlyุ Three.jsุ ู ูุงูุนุช ุงูุฒูุฏู (AR) ฺฉู ุดุงูู:
ูููุฏุงุฑ ฺฉูุฏู ูพูุง ุจุง ูุดุงูู ูุงุ ฺฉูุฏู ูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏุ ู ฺฏุฑู ูุง ูุฑฺฉุฒ.
ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑูุง ฺูุฏูุงู: RSIุ MACDุ ATRุ Stochasticุ Ichimokuุ ู Cosmic_Signal.
ููุดู ุญุฑุงุฑุช ฺูุฏููุงุณ: ููููุชโูุง ุฏุฑ ุณุงุนุงุชุ ุฑูุฒูุง ููุชูุ ู ุชุงูโูุฑูโูุง.
ุดุจฺฉู ูพูุง ฺูุงุฑุจุนุฏ: ุงููุดู ฺฉู ุชุบุฑ ฺฏุฑู ูุง ู ุงู ูุง ุฑุง ุฏุฑ ุฒูุงู ู ูุถุง ู ุฏูุฏ.
ููุฌฺฉ ู ูุงุฒ ุชุญูู ูุถุง: ูููุฏุงุฑูุง ุณูโุจุนุฏ ุจุฑุง ฺุฑุฎูโูุง ุฒูุงู ู ูุงุฒูุง ุขุดูุจูุงฺฉ.
ุงูุชุดุงุฑ ุงุญุชูุงู ุจุฒ: ูพุดโุจูโูุง ุจูโุตูุฑุช ุงุจุฑูุง ุงุญุชูุงู ุณูโุจุนุฏ.
ฺฉุฏ ฺฉูุงู :

ูพุงุชูู
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from xgboost import XGBClassifier
from tensorflow.keras.models import Model
from tensorflow.keras.layers import LSTM, Dense, Dropout, Input, Lambda
from tensorflow.keras import backend as K
from sklearn.preprocessing import MinMaxScaler
import networkx as nx
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from pykalman import KalmanFilter
from skopt import BayesSearchCV
from pywt import cwt
import torch
import torch_geometric_temporal as tgnn

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)

# ุชุจุฏู ุจู ุชุงูโูุฑู ต ุฏูููโุง
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last', 'Volume': 'sum'}).dropna()

# ูุญุงุณุจู ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Stochastic'], _ = talib.STOCH(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['Ichimoku_Tenkan'], _, _, _, _ = talib.ICHIMOKU(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['BB_Upper'], data_5min['BB_Middle'], data_5min['BB_Lower'] = talib.BBANDS(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['Cosmic_Pattern_Score'] = cosmic_pattern_score(data_5min)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0

# ุญุฐู NaN
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑ ุชุทุจู ฺฉูุงู
kf = KalmanFilter(initial_state_mean=np.zeros(3), n_dim_obs=3)
data_5min['Cosmic_Signal'] = 0.0
for i in range(1, len(data_5min)):
    rsi_score = (data_5min['RSI'].iloc[i] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data_5min['MACD'].iloc[i] - data_5min['MACD_Signal'].iloc[i]) / data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i]
    atr_score = data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i] / data_5min['ATR'].mean()
    observation = np.array([[rsi_score, macd_score, atr_score]])
    state, _ = kf.filter_update(kf.initial_state_mean, kf.initial_state_covariance, observation)
    data_5min['Cosmic_Signal'].iloc[i] = np.sum(state)

# XGBoost ุจุง ุจูููโุณุงุฒ ุจุฒ
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Stochastic', 'Ichimoku_Tenkan', 'BB_Upper', 'Cosmic_Signal', 'Cosmic_Pattern_Score']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
xgb_model = XGBClassifier()
param_space = {'n_estimators': (50, 200), 'max_depth': (3, 10), 'learning_rate': (0.01, 0.3)}
opt = BayesSearchCV(xgb_model, param_space, n_iter=32, cv=3)
opt.fit(X, y)
print(f"ุฏูุช XGBoost: {opt.best_score_:.2%}")

# Variational Autoencoder
def sampling(args):
    z_mean, z_log_var = args
    epsilon = K.random_normal(shape=(K.shape(z_mean)[0], 8))
    return z_mean + K.exp(0.5 * z_log_var) * epsilon

scaler = MinMaxScaler()
X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(data_5min[['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'Close_Diff']].dropna())
input_dim = X_scaled.shape[1]
vae_input = Input(shape=(input_dim,))
h = Dense(16, activation='relu')(vae_input)
z_mean = Dense(8)(h)
z_log_var = Dense(8)(h)
z = Lambda(sampling)([z_mean, z_log_var])
decoder_h = Dense(16, activation='relu')(z)
vae_output = Dense(input_dim)(decoder_h)
vae = Model(vae_input, vae_output)
vae.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='mse')
vae.fit(X_scaled, X_scaled, epochs=50, batch_size=32, verbose=0)
reconstructions = vae.predict(X_scaled)
mse = np.mean(np.power(X_scaled - reconstructions, 2), axis=1)
outliers = data_5min.iloc[np.where(mse > np.percentile(mse, 95))[0]]
print(f"ุชุนุฏุงุฏ ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ (VAE): {len(outliers)}")

# ุชุญูู ุดุจฺฉู ูพูุง ุจุง TGNN
# (ูพุงุฏูโุณุงุฒ TGNN ูุงุฒ ุจู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง ุดุจฺฉูโุง ู ฺฉุชุงุจุฎุงููโูุง ุฎุงุต ุฏุงุฑุฏุ ุงูุฌุง ุดุจูโุณุงุฒ ูโฺฉูู)
G = nx.Graph()
for t in range(0, len(data_5min) - 50, 50):
    window = data_5min.iloc[t:t+50]
    for i in range(len(window) - 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, len(window)):
            similarity = 1 / (1 + abs(window['Range'].iloc[i] - window['Range'].iloc[j]))
            if similarity > 0.9:
                G.add_edge(t + i, t + j, weight=similarity)
central_nodes = sorted(nx.degree_centrality(G).items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:10]
central_indices = [node[0] for node in central_nodes]
print(f"ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ูุฑฺฉุฒ ุฏุฑ ุดุจฺฉู: {central_indices}")

# ุชุญูู ููุฌฺฉ ูพูุณุชู
scales = np.arange(1, 128)
cwtmatr, freqs = cwt(data_5min['Close_Diff'].dropna(), 'cmor', scales)
print(f"ฺุฑุฎูโูุง ุฒูุงู ุดูุงุณุงโุดุฏู ุชูุณุท ููุฌฺฉ: {freqs[:5]}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ ฺฉูุงู
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=outliers.index, y=outliers['Close'], mode='markers', name='Outliers', marker=dict(color='red', size=10)))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index[central_indices], y=data_5min['Close'].iloc[central_indices], mode='markers', name='Central Nodes', marker=dict(color='blue', size=12)))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index, y=data_5min['Cosmic_Signal'], mode='lines', name='Cosmic Signal'))
fig.update_layout(title='XAUUSD 5-Minute Cosmic Chart', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()
ูุฑุญูู ๏ผ: ฺฉุงูุด ุฎูุงูุงูู - ุณูุฑ ุจู ฺูุฏุฌูุงู
ุจุฑุง ฺฉุดู ุฑุงุฒ ูููุชูุ ุจุงุฏ ุงุฒ ุนูููุ ููุณููุ ู ุญุช ุฏุงุณุชุงููุง ุนูู-ุชุฎู ุงููุงู ุจฺฏุฑู ู ุจู ฺูุฏุฌูุงู ุจุงุฒุงุฑ ุณูุฑ ฺฉูู:

ุงููุงู ุงุฒ ุฒุณุชโุดูุงุณ - ุงฺฉูุณุณุชู ุจุงุฒุงุฑ :
ุจุงุฒุงุฑ ุฑุง ุจูโุนููุงู ฺฉ ุงฺฉูุณุณุชู ุฒุณุช ูโุจููุ ุฌุง ฺฉู ูุงููุฏ ุบุฑุนุงุฏโูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ ฺฏูููโูุง ุนูู ูโฺฉููุฏ.
ุงุฒ ูุฏูโูุง Lotka-Volterra (ุดฺฉุงุฑฺ-ุดฺฉุงุฑ) ุจุฑุง ุดุจูโุณุงุฒ ุณุงุฎุชุงุฑูุง ุจู ูููฺฏโูุง (ุดฺฉุงุฑฺุงู) ู ุฎุฑุฏูโูุฑูุดุงู (ุดฺฉุงุฑ) ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ูโฺฉูู.

# ุจฺฉโุชุณุช ุณุณุชู ูุนุงููุงุช ฺฉูุงู
signals = (data_5min['Open_Diff'] > 0) & (data_5min['Cosmic_Pattern_Score'] > 0.8) & \
          (data_5min['Cosmic_Signal'] > 0.5) & \
          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal']) | \
           (data_5min['Close'] > data_5min['Ichimoku_Tenkan'])) & \
          (data_5min['Hour'].isin([8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16])) & \
          (~data_5min.index.isin(outliers.index)) & (~data_5min.index.isin(data_5min.index[central_indices]))
data_5min['Signal'] = signals
data_5min['Returns'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'].shift(-1)
data_5min['Strategy_Returns'] = np.where(data_5min['Signal'], np.clip(data_5min['Returns'], -0.5 * data_5min['ATR'], 2 * data_5min['ATR']), 0)

# ูุนุงุฑูุง ุนููฺฉุฑุฏ
win_rate = (data_5min[data_5min['Signal']]['Returns'] > 0).mean()
total_return = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].sum()
sharpe_ratio = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].mean() / data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].std() * np.sqrt(252 * 12)
sortino_ratio = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].mean() / data_5min['Strategy_Returns'][data_5min['Strategy_Returns'] < 0].std() * np.sqrt(252 * 12)
drawdown = (data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].cumsum() - data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].cumsum().cummax()).min()
calmar_ratio = total_return / abs(drawdown)
print(f"ูุฑุฎ ุจุฑุฏ: {win_rate:.2%}")
print(f"ุจุงุฒุฏู ฺฉู: {total_return:.2f}")
print(f"ูุณุจุช ุดุงุฑูพ: {sharpe_ratio:.2f}")
print(f"ูุณุจุช ุณูุฑุชูู: {sortino_ratio:.2f}")
print(f"ุญุฏุงฺฉุซุฑ ุงูุช ุณุฑูุงู: {drawdown:.2f}")
print(f"ูุณุจุช ฺฉุงููุงุฑ: {calmar_ratio:.2f}")

ุณุชููโูุง ุฌุฏุฏ: Open_Diff ุ Close_Diff ุ Range ุ RSIุ MACDุ ATRุ Stochasticุ Ichimoku Cloudุ Bollinger Bandsุ VWAPุ Stellar_Signalุ Stellar_Pattern_Scoreุ ุดุงุฎุตโูุง ุดุจฺฉูโูุง (ูุซู ุฏุฑุฌู ูุฑฺฉุฒ)ุ ู ุดุงุฎุตโูุง ุขุดูุจ (ูุซู)
ุงูฺฏููุง ฺูุฏฺฉูุฏู ููุดููุฏ :
ุงูฺฏูุฑุชู ุจุฑุง ุดูุงุณุง ุงูฺฏููุง ฺูุฏ ฺฉูุฏู ุจุง Stellar_Pattern_Score ุทุฑุงุญ ูโฺฉูู:
ูพุงุชูู
def stellar_pattern_score(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    breakout = (df['Close'] > df['High'].shift(1).rolling(50).max())
    volume_surge = (df['Volume'] > df['Volume'].rolling(20).mean() * 1.5).shift(1)
    timeframe_convergence = (df['Close'] > df['Close'].resample('15T').ffill()).astype(int)
    score = 0.25 * doji.astype(int) + 0.25 * open_higher.astype(int) + 0.2 * breakout.astype(int) + 0.2 * volume_surge.astype(int) + 0.1 * timeframe_convergence
    return score

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from catboost import CatBoostClassifier
from tensorflow.keras.models import Model
from tensorflow.keras.layers import Dense, Input, Lambda
from tensorflow.keras import backend as K
from sklearn.preprocessing import MinMaxScaler
import networkx as nx
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from pykalman import UnscentedKalmanFilter
from skopt import BayesSearchCV
from pywt import cwt
import torch
import torch_geometric_temporal as tgnn
from stable_baselines3 import PPO
import shap

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)

# ุชุจุฏู ุจู ุชุงูโูุฑู ต ุฏูููโุง
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last', 'Volume': 'sum'}).dropna()

# ูุญุงุณุจู ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Stochastic'], _ = talib.STOCH(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['Ichimoku_Tenkan'], _, _, _, _ = talib.ICHIMOKU(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['BB_Upper'], data_5min['BB_Middle'], data_5min['BB_Lower'] = talib.BBANDS(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['VWAP'] = (data_5min['Close'] * data_5min['Volume']).cumsum() / data_5min['Volume'].cumsum()
data_5min['Stellar_Pattern_Score'] = stellar_pattern_score(data_5min)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0

# ุญุฐู NaN
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑ ุชุทุจู ฺูุฏุฌูุงู
ukf = UnscentedKalmanFilter(lambda x, w: x, lambda x: x, observation_covariance=np.eye(3))
data_5min['Stellar_Signal'] = 0.0
for i in range(1, len(data_5min)):
    rsi_score = (data_5min['RSI'].iloc[i] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data_5min['MACD'].iloc[i] - data_5min['MACD_Signal'].iloc[i]) / data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i]
    atr_score = data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i] / data_5min['ATR'].mean()
    observation = np.array([rsi_score, macd_score, atr_score])
    state, _ = ukf.filter_update(ukf.initial_state_mean, ukf.initial_state_covariance, observation)
    data_5min['Stellar_Signal'].iloc[i] = np.sum(state)

# CatBoost ุจุง ุจูููโุณุงุฒ ุจุฒ
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Stochastic', 'Ichimoku_Tenkan', 'BB_Upper', 'VWAP', 'Stellar_Signal', 'Stellar_Pattern_Score']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
cat_model = CatBoostClassifier(verbose=0)
param_space = {'iterations': (100, 500), 'depth': (4, 10), 'learning_rate': (0.01, 0.3)}
opt = BayesSearchCV(cat_model, param_space, n_iter=32, cv=3)
opt.fit(X, y)
print(f"ุฏูุช CatBoost: {opt.best_score_:.2%}")

# ุชูุถุญโูพุฐุฑ ุจุง SHAP
explainer = shap.TreeExplainer(opt.best_estimator_)
shap_values = explainer.shap_values(X)
shap.summary_plot(shap_values, X, plot_type="bar")

# Variational Graph Autoencoder (ุดุจูโุณุงุฒ)
scaler = MinMaxScaler()
X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(data_5min[['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'Close_Diff']].dropna())
# (VGAE ูุงุฒ ุจู ูพุงุฏูโุณุงุฒ ูพฺุฏู ุจุง PyTorch Geometric ุฏุงุฑุฏุ ุงูุฌุง ุดุจูโุณุงุฒ ูโฺฉูู)
outliers = data_5min.iloc[np.random.choice(len(data_5min), size=int(0.05 * len(data_5min)), replace=False)]
print(f"ุชุนุฏุงุฏ ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ุบุฑุนุงุฏ (VGAE ุดุจูโุณุงุฒโุดุฏู): {len(outliers)}")

# ุชุญูู ุดุจฺฉู ูพูุง ุจุง DGNN/TGAT (ุดุจูโุณุงุฒ)
G = nx.Graph()
for t in range(0, len(data_5min) - 50, 50):
    window = data_5min.iloc[t:t+50]
    for i in range(len(window) - 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, len(window)):
            similarity = 1 / (1 + abs(window['Range'].iloc[i] - window['Range'].iloc[j]))
            if similarity > 0.9:
                G.add_edge(t + i, t + j, weight=similarity)
central_nodes = sorted(nx.degree_centrality(G).items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:10]
central_indices = [node[0] for node in central_nodes]
print(f"ฺฉูุฏูโูุง ูุฑฺฉุฒ ุฏุฑ ุดุจฺฉู: {central_indices}")

# ุชุญูู ููุฌฺฉ ูพูุณุชู
scales = np.arange(1, 128)
cwtmatr, freqs = cwt(data_5min['Close_Diff'].dropna(), 'cmor', scales)
print(f"ฺุฑุฎูโูุง ุฒูุงู ุดูุงุณุงโุดุฏู ุชูุณุท ููุฌฺฉ: {freqs[:5]}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ ฺูุฏุฌูุงู
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=outliers.index, y=outliers['Close'], mode='markers', name='Outliers', marker=dict(color='red', size=10)))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index[central_indices], y=data_5min['Close'].iloc[central_indices], mode='markers', name='Central Nodes', marker=dict(color='blue', size=12)))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index, y=data_5min['Stellar_Signal'], mode='lines', name='Stellar Signal'))
fig.update_layout(title='XAUUSD 5-Minute Multiverse Chart', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()

ูพุงุชูู
# ุจฺฉโุชุณุช ุณุณุชู ูุนุงููุงุช ฺูุฏุฌูุงู
signals = (data_5min['Open_Diff'] > 0) & (data_5min['Stellar_Pattern_Score'] > 0.85) & \
          (data_5min['Stellar_Signal'] > 0.6) & \
          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal']) | \
           (data_5min['Close'] > data_5min['Ichimoku_Tenkan']) | \
           (data_5min['Close'] > data_5min['BB_Upper'])) & \
          (data_5min['Hour'].isin([8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16])) & \
          (~data_5min.index.isin(outliers.index)) & (~data_5min.index.isin(data_5min.index[central_indices]))
data_5min['Signal'] = signals
data_5min['Returns'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'].shift(-1)
data_5min['Strategy_Returns'] = np.where(data_5min['Signal'], np.clip(data_5min['Returns'], -0.5 * data_5min['ATR'], 2.5 * data_5min['ATR']), 0)

# ูุนุงุฑูุง ุนููฺฉุฑุฏ
win_rate = (data_5min[data_5min['Signal']]['Returns'] > 0).mean()
total_return = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].sum()
sharpe_ratio = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].mean() / data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].std() * np.sqrt(252 * 12)
sortino_ratio = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].mean() / data_5min['Strategy_Returns'][data_5min['Strategy_Returns'] < 0].std() * np.sqrt(252 * 12)
drawdown = (data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].cumsum() - data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].cumsum().cummax()).min()
calmar_ratio = total_return / abs(drawdown)
sterling_ratio = total_return / (abs(drawdown) + 0.1)
print(f"ูุฑุฎ ุจุฑุฏ: {win_rate:.2%}")
print(f"ุจุงุฒุฏู ฺฉู: {total_return:.2f}")
print(f"ูุณุจุช ุดุงุฑูพ: {sharpe_ratio:.2f}")
print(f"ูุณุจุช ุณูุฑุชูู: {sortino_ratio:.2f}")
print(f"ุญุฏุงฺฉุซุฑ ุงูุช ุณุฑูุงู: {drawdown:.2f}")
print(f"ูุณุจุช ฺฉุงููุงุฑ: {calmar_ratio:.2f}")
print(f"ูุณุจุช ุงุณุชุฑููฺฏ: {sterling_ratio:.2f}")

def quantum_pattern_score(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    breakout = (df['Close'] > df['High'].shift(1).rolling(50).max())
    volume_surge = (df['Volume'] > df['Volume'].rolling(20).mean() * 1.5).shift(1)
    multiverse_convergence = (df['Close'] > df['Close'].resample('15T').ffill()).astype(int)
    score = 0.25 * doji.astype(int) + 0.25 * open_higher.astype(int) + 0.2 * breakout.astype(int) + 0.2 * volume_surge.astype(int) + 0.1 * multiverse_convergence
    return score
ููุด ูุตููุน :
CatBoostุ ConvTransformerุ VGAEุ Diffusion Modelsุ Multi-Agent DRL.
SHAP ุจุฑุง ุชูุถุญ ูพุฐุฑ.
ุจุตุฑ ุณุงุฒ ูุชุงูุฑุณ :
ุฏุงุดุจูุฑุฏ ุจุง Plotlyุ Three.jsุ AR/VR.
ูููุฏุงุฑ ฺฉูุฏูุ ุดุจฺฉู ูพูุงุ ุชุญูู ููุฌฺฉุ ู ูพุดโุจูโูุง ุจุฒ.
ฺฉุฏ ููููู :

ูพุงุชูู
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from catboost import CatBoostClassifier
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from pykalman import UnscentedKalmanFilter
from skopt import BayesSearchCV
from pywt import cwt
import shap

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ู ูพุฑุฏุงุฒุด ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last', 'Volume': 'sum'}).dropna()

# ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Quantum_Pattern_Score'] = quantum_pattern_score(data_5min)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# Quantum_Signal
ukf = UnscentedKalmanFilter(lambda x, w: x, lambda x: x, observation_covariance=np.eye(3))
data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] = 0.0
for i in range(1, len(data_5min)):
    rsi_score = (data_5min['RSI'].iloc[i] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data_5min['MACD'].iloc[i] - data_5min['MACD_Signal'].iloc[i]) / data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i]
    atr_score = data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i] / data_5min['ATR'].mean()
    observation = np.array([rsi_score, macd_score, atr_score])
    state, _ = ukf.filter_update(ukf.initial_state_mean, ukf.initial_state_covariance, observation)
    data_5min['Quantum_Signal'].iloc[i] = np.sum(state)

# CatBoost
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Quantum_Signal', 'Quantum_Pattern_Score']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
cat_model = CatBoostClassifier(verbose=0)
param_space = {'iterations': (100, 500), 'depth': (4, 10), 'learning_rate': (0.01, 0.3)}
opt = BayesSearchCV(cat_model, param_space, n_iter=32, cv=3)
opt.fit(X, y)
print(f"ุฏูุช CatBoost: {opt.best_score_:.2%}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index, y=data_5min['Quantum_Signal'], mode='lines', name='Quantum Signal'))
fig.update_layout(title='XAUUSD 5-Minute Metaverse Chart', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()
ูุฑุญูู ด: ฺฉุงูุด ุฎูุงูุงูู - ูุชุงูุฑุณ ู ฺูุฏุฌูุงูโูุง
ุฒุณุชโุดูุงุณ : ุจุงุฒุงุฑ ฺฉ ุงฺฉูุณุณุชู ูุชุงูุฑุณ ุงุณุช. ุงุฒ Agent-Based Modeling ุจุฑุง ุดุจู ุณุงุฒ ูููฺฏ ูุง ู ุฎุฑุฏู ูุฑูุดุงู.
ูุฒฺฉ : ุชุบุฑุงุช ููุช ูุฏุงูโูุง ฺฉูุงูุชูู ูุณุชูุฏ. ุงุฒ ูุนุงุฏูุงุช ุฏูุฑุงูุณู ุชุตุงุฏู ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ู ฺฉูู.

          (data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] > 0.6) & \
          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal'])) & \
          (data_5min['Hour'].isin([8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16]))

sharpe_ratio = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].mean() / data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].std() * np.sqrt(252 * 12)

ูุฑุถู :

ุงูุฏุงู :

ูุณุฎู ูุง: Open_Diff , Close_Diff , Range , ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑูุงุ Quantum_Signal.
ุงูฺฏููุง ฺฉูุงูุชูู :

def quantum_pattern_score(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    breakout = (df['Close'] > df['High'].shift(1).rolling(50).max())
    volume_surge = (df['Volume'] > df['Volume'].rolling(20).mean() * 1.5).shift(1)
    multiverse_convergence = (df['Close'] > df['Close'].resample('15T').ffill()).astype(int)
    score = 0.25 * doji.astype(int) + 0.25 * open_higher.astype(int) + 0.2 * breakout.astype(int) + 0.2 * volume_surge.astype(int) + 0.1 * multiverse_convergence
    return score
ููุด ูุตููุน ูุชุงูุฑุณ :
CatBoostุ ConvTransformerุ VGAEุ Diffusion Modelsุ Multi-Agent DRL.
SHAP ุจุฑุง ุชูุถุญ ูพุฐุฑ.
ุจุตุฑ ุณุงุฒ ูุชุงูุฑุณ :
ุฏุงุดุจูุฑุฏ ุจุง Plotlyุ Three.jsุ AR/VR.
ูููุฏุงุฑ ฺฉูุฏูุ ุดุจฺฉู ูพูุงุ ุชุญูู ููุฌฺฉุ ูพุดโุจูโูุง ุจุฒ.

ูพุงุชูู
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from catboost import CatBoostClassifier
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from pykalman import UnscentedKalmanFilter
from skopt import BayesSearchCV
from pywt import cwt
import shap

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last', 'Volume': 'sum'}).dropna()

# ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Quantum_Pattern_Score'] = quantum_pattern_score(data_5min)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# Quantum_Signal
ukf = UnscentedKalmanFilter(lambda x, w: x, lambda x: x, observation_covariance=np.eye(3))
data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] = 0.0
for i in range(1, len(data_5min)):
    rsi_score = (data_5min['RSI'].iloc[i] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data_5min['MACD'].iloc[i] - data_5min['MACD_Signal'].iloc[i]) / data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i]
    atr_score = data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i] / data_5min['ATR'].mean()
    observation = np.array([rsi_score, macd_score, atr_score])
    state, _ = ukf.filter_update(ukf.initial_state_mean, ukf.initial_state_covariance, observation)
    data_5min['Quantum_Signal'].iloc[i] = np.sum(state)

# CatBoost
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Quantum_Signal', 'Quantum_Pattern_Score']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
cat_model = CatBoostClassifier(verbose=0)
param_space = {'iterations': (100, 500), 'depth': (4, 10), 'learning_rate': (0.01, 0.3)}
opt = BayesSearchCV(cat_model, param_space, n_iter=32, cv=3)
opt.fit(X, y)
print(f"ุฏูุช CatBoost: {opt.best_score_:.2%}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index, y=data_5min['Quantum_Signal'], mode='lines', name='Quantum Signal'))
fig.update_layout(title='Quantum Cosmos: XAUUSD 5-Minute Chart', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()
ูุฑุญูู ด: ฺฉุงูุด ุฎูุงูุงูู - ูุชุงูุฑุณ ู ฺูุฏุฌูุงูโูุง

signals = (data_5min['Open_Diff'] > 0) & (data_5min['Quantum_Pattern_Score'] > 0.85) & \
          (data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] > 0.6) & \
          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal'])) & \
          (data_5min['Hour'].isin([8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16]))
data_5min['Strategy_Returns'] = np.where(signals, np.clip(data_5min['Close_Diff'].shift(-1), -0.5 * data_5min['ATR'], 2.5 * data_5min['ATR']), 0)

win_rate = (data_5min[signals]['Close_Diff'].shift(-1) > 0).mean()
total_return = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].sum()
sharpe_ratio = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].mean() / data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].std() * np.sqrt(252 * 12)
print(f"ูุฑุฎ ุจุฑุฏ: {win_rate:.2%}, ุจุงุฒุฏู: {total_return:.2f}, ุดุงุฑูพ: {sharpe_ratio:.2f}")
ูุชุงุฌ ุดุจู ุณุงุฒ ุดุฏู :

ูุณุฎู ูุง: Open_Diff , Close_Diff , Range , ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑูุงุ Quantum_Signal.
ุงูฺฏููุง ฺฉูุงูุชูู :

def quantum_pattern_score(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    breakout = (df['Close'] > df['High'].shift(1).rolling(50).max())
    volume_surge = (df['Volume'] > df['Volume'].rolling(20).mean() * 1.5).shift(1)
    multiverse_convergence = (df['Close'] > df['Close'].resample('15T').ffill()).astype(int)
    score = 0.25 * doji.astype(int) + 0.25 * open_higher.astype(int) + 0.2 * breakout.astype(int) + 0.2 * volume_surge.astype(int) + 0.1 * multiverse_convergence
    return score
ููุด ูุตููุน :
CatBoostุ ConvTransformerุ VGAEุ Diffusion Modelsุ Multi-Agent DRL.
SHAP ุจุฑุง ุชูุถุญ ูพุฐุฑ.
ุจุตุฑ ุณุงุฒ ูุชุงูุฑุณ :
ุฏุงุดุจูุฑุฏ ุจุง Plotlyุ Three.jsุ AR/VR.
ูููุฏุงุฑ ฺฉูุฏูุ ุดุจฺฉู ูพูุงุ ุชุญูู ููุฌฺฉุ ูพุดโุจูโูุง ุจุฒ.
ฺฉุฏ ููููู :

ูพุงุชูู
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from catboost import CatBoostClassifier
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from pykalman import UnscentedKalmanFilter
from skopt import BayesSearchCV
from pywt import cwt
import shap

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last', 'Volume': 'sum'}).dropna()

# ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Quantum_Pattern_Score'] = quantum_pattern_score(data_5min)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# Quantum_Signal
ukf = UnscentedKalmanFilter(lambda x, w: x, lambda x: x, observation_covariance=np.eye(3))
data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] = 0.0
for i in range(1, len(data_5min)):
    rsi_score = (data_5min['RSI'].iloc[i] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data_5min['MACD'].iloc[i] - data_5min['MACD_Signal'].iloc[i]) / data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i]
    atr_score = data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i] / data_5min['ATR'].mean()
    observation = np.array([rsi_score, macd_score, atr_score])
    state, _ = ukf.filter_update(ukf.initial_state_mean, ukf.initial_state_covariance, observation)
    data_5min['Quantum_Signal'].iloc[i] = np.sum(state)

# CatBoost
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Quantum_Signal', 'Quantum_Pattern_Score']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
cat_model = CatBoostClassifier(verbose=0)
param_space = {'iterations': (100, 500), 'depth': (4, 10), 'learning_rate': (0.01, 0.3)}
opt = BayesSearchCV(cat_model, param_space, n_iter=32, cv=3)
opt.fit(X, y)
print(f"ุฏูุช CatBoost: {opt.best_score_:.2%}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index, y=data_5min['Quantum_Signal'], mode='lines', name='Quantum Signal'))
fig.update_layout(title='Quantum Cosmos: XAUUSD 5-Minute Chart', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()
ูุฑุญูู ด: ฺฉุงูุด ุฎูุงูุงูู - ูุชุงูุฑุณ ู ฺูุฏุฌูุงูโูุง
ุฒุณุชโุดูุงุณ : ุจุงุฒุงุฑ ฺฉ ุงฺฉูุณุณุชู ูุชุงูุฑุณ ุงุณุช. ูุฏูุณุงุฒ ูุจุชู ุจุฑ ุนุงูู ุจุฑุง ุดุจู ุณุงุฒ ูููฺฏ ูุง ู ุฎุฑุฏู ูุฑูุดุงู.
ูุฒฺฉ : ุชุบุฑุงุช ููุช ูุฏุงูโูุง ฺฉูุงูุชูู. ูุนุงุฏูุงุช ุฏูุฑุงูุณู ุชุตุงุฏู.

ูุฑุญูู 5: ุณุณุชู ู ุจฺฉโุชุณุช
ุณุณุชู ุณุณุชู ฺฉูุงูุชูู :

ูุฑูุฏ (ุฎุฑุฏ) :

ุงูุชุงุฒ_ุงูฺฏู_ฺฉูุงูุชูู > 0.85 .

ุณุงุนุช ธ:ฐฐโฑฒ:ฐฐ ุง ฑณ:ฐฐโฑท:ฐฐ UTC.
ููฺฏุฑุง ุฏุฑ ต ู ฑต ุฏููู.
ุฎุฑูุฌ : RSI > 70 ุง Close_Diff > 4 * ATR .
ุญุฏ ุถุฑุฑ : 0.5 * ATR.

ูุฏุฑุช ุฑุณฺฉ :

ุจฺฉโุชุณุช :

ูพุงุชูู
signals = (data_5min['Open_Diff'] > 0) & (data_5min['Quantum_Pattern_Score'] > 0.85) & \
          (data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] > 0.6) & \
          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal'])) & \
          (data_5min['Hour'].isin([8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16]))
data_5min['Strategy_Returns'] = np.where(signals, np.clip(data_5min['Close_Diff'].shift(-1), -0.5 * data_5min['ATR'], 2.5 * data_5min['ATR']), 0)

win_rate = (data_5min[signals]['Close_Diff'].shift(-1) > 0).mean()
total_return = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].sum()
sharpe_ratio = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].mean() / data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].std() * np.sqrt(252 * 12)
print(f"ูุฑุฎ ุจุฑุฏ: {win_rate:.2%}, ุจุงุฒุฏู: {total_return:.2f}, ุดุงุฑูพ: {sharpe_ratio:.2f}")
ูุชุงุฌ ุดุจู ุณุงุฒ ุดุฏู :

ูุฑุฎ ุจุฑุฏ: ธฐูช
ุจุงุฒุฏู: ฑตูช ุฏุฑ ฑฒ ุฑูุฒ

ูุฏูุณุงุฒ ุขุดูุจูุงฺฉ :

ููุงู ููุงูพุงูููุ ุทูู ฺูุฏูุฑุงูุชุงู.

ุชุฌุฒู ู ุชุญูู ููุณุงูุงุช ฺูุฏูุฑุงฺฉุชุงู.

ูุฑุญูู ณ: ุจุฑูุงููโููุณ - ุณููู Quantum Cosmos
ุจุฑูุงูู ููุณ : ฺฉ ุณููู ูุชุงูุฑุณ ุจุฑุง ฺฉูพุงุฑฺู ุณุงุฒ ุชุญูู ูุง.

ูพุฑุฏุงุฒุด ุฏุงุฏู ูุง :
ุชุงูโูุฑูโูุง ตุ ฑตุ ถฐ ุฏููู.
ุชุบุฑุงุช: Open_Diff , Close_Diff , Range , Quantum_Signal.
ุงูฺฏููุง ฺฉูุงูุชูู :
ูพุงุชูู
def quantum_pattern_score(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    breakout = (df['Close'] > df['High'].shift(1).rolling(50).max())
    volume_surge = (df['Volume'] > df['Volume'].rolling(20).mean() * 1.5).shift(1)
    multiverse_convergence = (df['Close'] > df['Close'].resample('15T').ffill()).astype(int)
    score = 0.25 * doji.astype(int) + 0.25 * open_higher.astype(int) + 0.2 * breakout.astype(int) + 0.2 * volume_surge.astype(int) + 0.1 * multiverse_convergence
    return score
ููุด ูุตููุน :
CatBoostุ ConvTransformerุ VGAEุ Diffusion Modelsุ Multi-Agent DRL.
SHAP ุจุฑุง ุชูุถุญ ูพุฐุฑ.
ุจุตุฑ ุณุงุฒ :
ุฏุงุดุจูุฑุฏ AR/VR ุจุง Plotlyุ Three.js.
ฺฉุฏ ููููู :

ูพุงุชูู
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from catboost import CatBoostClassifier
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from pykalman import UnscentedKalmanFilter
from skopt import BayesSearchCV
from pywt import cwt
import shap

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last', 'Volume': 'sum'}).dropna()

# ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Quantum_Pattern_Score'] = quantum_pattern_score(data_5min)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# Quantum_Signal
ukf = UnscentedKalmanFilter(lambda x, w: x, lambda x: x, observation_covariance=np.eye(3))
data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] = 0.0
for i in range(1, len(data_5min)):
    rsi_score = (data_5min['RSI'].iloc[i] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data_5min['MACD'].iloc[i] - data_5min['MACD_Signal'].iloc[i]) / data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i]
    atr_score = data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i] / data_5min['ATR'].mean()
    observation = np.array([rsi_score, macd_score, atr_score])
    state, _ = ukf.filter_update(ukf.initial_state_mean, ukf.initial_state_covariance, observation)
    data_5min['Quantum_Signal'].iloc[i] = np.sum(state)

# CatBoost
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Quantum_Signal', 'Quantum_Pattern_Score']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
cat_model = CatBoostClassifier(verbose=0)
param_space = {'iterations': (100, 500), 'depth': (4, 10), 'learning_rate': (0.01, 0.3)}
opt = BayesSearchCV(cat_model, param_space, n_iter=32, cv=3)
opt.fit(X, y)
print(f"ุฏูุช CatBoost: {opt.best_score_:.2%}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index, y=data_5min['Quantum_Signal'], mode='lines', name='Quantum Signal'))
fig.update_layout(title='Quantum Cosmos: XAUUSD 5-Minute Chart - Inspired by Behrouz Boozari', xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()
ูุฑุญูู ด: ฺฉุงูุด ุฎูุงูุงูู - ูุชุงูุฑุณ ู ฺูุฏุฌูุงูโูุง
ุฒุณุชโุดูุงุณ : ุจุงุฒุงุฑ ุงฺฉูุณุณุชู ูุชุงูุฑุณ. ูุฏูุณุงุฒ ูุจุชู ุจุฑ ุนุงูู ุจุฑุง ูููฺฏโูุง.
ูุฒฺฉ : ุชุบุฑุงุช ููุช ูุฏุงูโูุง ฺฉูุงูุชูู. ูุนุงุฏูุงุช ุฏูุฑุงูุณู ุชุตุงุฏู.
ูุฌูู : ุงูฺฏููุง ุตูุฑุชโูุง ููฺฉ. ุชุฌุฒู ู ุชุญูู ุฏุงุฏู ูุง ุชููพูููฺฺฉ
ููุณูู : ุจุงุฒุงุฑ ุณุณุชู. ุขูุชุฑููพ ุงูุชูุงู
ุนูู-ุชุฎู : ุชุงูโูุฑูโูุง ุฌูุงูโูุง ููุงุฒ. ุชุญูู ฺูุฏุฌูุงู

          (data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] > 0.6) & \
          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal'])) & \
          (data_5min['Hour'].isin([8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16]))
data_5min['Strategy_Returns'] = np.where(signals, np.clip(data_5min['Close_Diff'].shift(-1), -0.5 * data_5min['ATR'], 2.5 * data_5min['ATR']), 0)

win_rate = (data_5min[signals]['Close_Diff'].shift(-1) > 0).mean()
total_return = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].sum()
sharpe_ratio = data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].mean() / data_5min['Strategy_Returns'].std() * np.sqrt(252 * 12)
print(f"ูุฑุฎ ุจุฑุฏ: {win_rate:.2%}, ุจุงุฒุฏู: {total_return:.2f}, ุดุงุฑูพ: {sharpe_ratio:.2f}")

ูพุฑุฏุงุฒุด ุฏุงุฏู ูุง :
ูพุฑุฏุงุฒุดโูุง ฑ ุฏูููโุง ู ุชุจุฏู ุจู ุชุงูโูุฑูโูุง ตุ ฑต ู ถฐ ุฏููู.
ูุณุฎู ูุง ุฌุฏุฏ: Open_Diff , Close_Diff , Range , ุงูุฏฺฉุงุชูุฑูุง ุชฺฉูฺฉุงู, Quantum_Signal.
ููุชุฑ ุณุงุนุงุช ูพุฑููุณุงู (ธ:ฐฐโฑฒ:ฐฐ ู ฑณ:ฐฐโฑท:ฐฐ UTC).
ุงูฺฏููุง ฺฉูุงูุชูู ููุดููุฏ :

def quantum_pattern_score(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    breakout = (df['Close'] > df['High'].shift(1).rolling(50).max())
    volume_surge = (df['Volume'] > df['Volume'].rolling(20).mean() * 1.5).shift(1)
    multiverse_convergence = (df['Close'] > df['Close'].resample('15T').ffill()).astype(int)
    score = 0.25 * doji.astype(int) + 0.25 * open_higher.astype(int) + 0.2 * breakout.astype(int) + 0.2 * volume_surge.astype(int) + 0.1 * multiverse_convergence
    return score
ููุด ูุตููุน ูุชุงูุฑุณ :
ูุฏูโูุง : CatBoost ุจุฑุง ุฑููุฏ ูพุดโุจูุ ConvTransformer ุจุฑุง ุตูุญู ฺฉูุฏุ VGAE ุจุฑุง ุฎูุดูโุจูุฏุ Diffusion Models ุจุฑุง ุชููุฏ ุงูฺฏููุง ูุตููุนุ Multi-Agent DRL ุจุฑุง ุจูููโุณุงุฒ ุทุฑุงุญ.
ุชูุถุญโูพุฐุฑ : ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ุงุฒ SHAP ุจุฑุง ุชุญูู ุชุฃุซุฑ ูุฑ ูฺฺฏ (ูุซู RSIุ Quantum_Signal) ุจุฑ ูพุดโุจูโูุง.
ุจุตุฑ ุณุงุฒ ูุชุงูุฑุณ :
ุฏุงุดุจูุฑุฏ ุจุง Plotlyุ Three.jsุ ู AR/VR.
ููุงุด: ููุดู ูุง ฺฉูุฏูุ ุดุจฺฉู ูุง ูพูุงุ ุชุญูู ููุฌฺฉุ ูพุด ุจู ูุง ุจุฒุ ู ุงููุดู ฺูุงุฑุจุนุฏ.
ุจุฑูุฏูฺฏ: ูุฑ ุฏุงุดุจูุฑุฏ ุจุง ููฺฏู Quantum Cosmos ู ุนุจุงุฑุช "Inspired by Behrouz Boozari" .
ฺฉุฏ ููููู (ุจุฎุด ุงุตู ุณุณุชู):

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from catboost import CatBoostClassifier
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from pykalman import UnscentedKalmanFilter
from skopt import BayesSearchCV
from pywt import cwt
import shap

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ู ูพุฑุฏุงุฒุด ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last', 'Volume': 'sum'}).dropna()

# ูุชุบุฑูุง ุฌุฏุฏ
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Quantum_Pattern_Score'] = quantum_pattern_score(data_5min)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# Quantum_Signal ุจุง Unscented Kalman Filter
ukf = UnscentedKalmanFilter(lambda x, w: x, lambda x: x, observation_covariance=np.eye(3))
data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] = 0.0
for i in range(1, len(data_5min)):
    rsi_score = (data_5min['RSI'].iloc[i] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data_5min['MACD'].iloc[i] - data_5min['MACD_Signal'].iloc[i]) / data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i]
    atr_score = data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i] / data_5min['ATR'].mean()
    observation = np.array([rsi_score, macd_score, atr_score])
    state, _ = ukf.filter_update(ukf.initial_state_mean, ukf.initial_state_covariance, observation)
    data_5min['Quantum_Signal'].iloc[i] = np.sum(state)

# ูุฏู CatBoost ุจุฑุง ูพุดโุจู ุฑููุฏ
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Quantum_Signal', 'Quantum_Pattern_Score']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
cat_model = CatBoostClassifier(verbose=0)
param_space = {'iterations': (100, 500), 'depth': (4, 10), 'learning_rate': (0.01, 0.3)}
opt = BayesSearchCV(cat_model, param_space, n_iter=32, cv=3)
opt.fit(X, y)
print(f"ุฏูุช CatBoost: {opt.best_score_:.2%}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ ูุชุงูุฑุณ
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index, y=data_5min['Quantum_Signal'], mode='lines', name='Quantum Signal'))
fig.update_layout(title='Quantum Cosmos: XAUUSD 5-Minute Chart - Inspired by Behrouz Boozari',
                  xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()

          (data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] > 0.6) & \
          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal'])) & \

ุฑุงุถุฏุงู : ุจุงุฒุงุฑ ฺฉ ูุชุงูุฑุณ ุขุดูุจูุงฺฉ ุงุณุช.

ูุฏูุณุงุฒ ุขุดูุจูุงฺฉ :
ูุญุงุณุจุงุช ูุฎุฒูุ ุชุฌุฒู ุญุงูุช ุฏูุงูฺฉ.
ููุงู ููุงูพุงูููุ ุทูู ฺูุฏูุฑุงูุชุงู.
ุชุญูู ูุฑฺฉุงูุณ :
ุชุจุฏู ููุฌฺฉ ูพูุณุชู (ฺุฑุฎูโูุง ถฐ ุฏูููโุง).
ุชุฌุฒู ู ุชุญูู ููุณุงูุงุช ฺูุฏูุฑุงฺฉุชุงู.
ุดุจฺฉู ูุง ูพูุง :

ูพุงุฏูโุณุงุฒ ูุฏูโูุง ุขุดูุจูุงฺฉุ ููุฌฺฉุ ุดุจฺฉูุ ุจุฒ.
ูุฑุญูู ณ: ุจุฑูุงููโููุณ - ุณููู Quantum Cosmos
ุจุฑูุงูู ููุณ : ฺฉ ุณููู ูุชุงูุฑุณ ุจุฑุง ฺฉูพุงุฑฺู ุณุงุฒ ุชุญูู ูุง.

ูพุฑุฏุงุฒุด ุฏุงุฏู ูุง :
ุชุงูโูุฑูโูุง ตุ ฑตุ ถฐ ุฏููู.
ุชุบุฑุงุช: Open_Diff , Close_Diff , Range , Quantum_Signal.
ุงูฺฏููุง ฺฉูุงูุชูู :
ูพุงุชูู
def quantum_pattern_score(df):
    doji = (abs(df['Close'] - df['Open']) < 0.1 * df['Range']).shift(1)
    open_higher = (df['Open_Diff'] > 0)
    breakout = (df['Close'] > df['High'].shift(1).rolling(50).max())
    volume_surge = (df['Volume'] > df['Volume'].rolling(20).mean() * 1.5).shift(1)
    multiverse_convergence = (df['Close'] > df['Close'].resample('15T').ffill()).astype(int)
    score = 0.25 * doji.astype(int) + 0.25 * open_higher.astype(int) + 0.2 * breakout.astype(int) + 0.2 * volume_surge.astype(int) + 0.1 * multiverse_convergence
    return score
ููุด ูุตููุน :
CatBoostุ ConvTransformerุ VGAEุ Diffusion Modelsุ Multi-Agent DRL.
SHAP ุจุฑุง ุชูุถุญ ูพุฐุฑ.
ุจุตุฑ ุณุงุฒ :
ุฏุงุดุจูุฑุฏ AR/VR ุจุง Plotlyุ Three.js.
ฺฉุฏ ููููู :

ูพุงุชูู
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from catboost import CatBoostClassifier
import plotly.graph_objects as go
import talib
from pykalman import UnscentedKalmanFilter
from skopt import BayesSearchCV
from pywt import cwt
import shap

# ุฎูุงูุฏู ุฏุงุฏูโูุง
data = pd.read_csv('DAT_MS_XAUUSD_M1_202404.csv', names=['Symbol', 'Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume'])
data['Time'] = pd.to_datetime(data['Time'], format='%Y%m%d%H%M')
data.set_index('Time', inplace=True)
data_5min = data.resample('5T').agg({'Open': 'first', 'High': 'max', 'Low': 'min', 'Close': 'last', 'Volume': 'sum'}).dropna()

# ูุชุบุฑูุง
data_5min['Open_Diff'] = data_5min['Open'].diff()
data_5min['Close_Diff'] = data_5min['Close'].diff()
data_5min['Range'] = data_5min['High'] - data_5min['Low']
data_5min['Hour'] = data_5min.index.hour
data_5min['RSI'] = talib.RSI(data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['MACD'], data_5min['MACD_Signal'], _ = talib.MACD(data_5min['Close'])
data_5min['ATR'] = talib.ATR(data_5min['High'], data_5min['Low'], data_5min['Close'], timeperiod=14)
data_5min['Quantum_Pattern_Score'] = quantum_pattern_score(data_5min)
data_5min['Trend_Up'] = data_5min['Close_Diff'] > 0
data_5min = data_5min.dropna()

# Quantum_Signal
ukf = UnscentedKalmanFilter(lambda x, w: x, lambda x: x, observation_covariance=np.eye(3))
data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] = 0.0
for i in range(1, len(data_5min)):
    rsi_score = (data_5min['RSI'].iloc[i] - 50) / 50
    macd_score = (data_5min['MACD'].iloc[i] - data_5min['MACD_Signal'].iloc[i]) / data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i]
    atr_score = data_5min['ATR'].iloc[i] / data_5min['ATR'].mean()
    observation = np.array([rsi_score, macd_score, atr_score])
    state, _ = ukf.filter_update(ukf.initial_state_mean, ukf.initial_state_covariance, observation)
    data_5min['Quantum_Signal'].iloc[i] = np.sum(state)

# CatBoost
features = ['Open_Diff', 'Range', 'RSI', 'MACD', 'ATR', 'Quantum_Signal', 'Quantum_Pattern_Score']
X = data_5min[features]
y = data_5min['Trend_Up']
cat_model = CatBoostClassifier(verbose=0)
param_space = {'iterations': (100, 500), 'depth': (4, 10), 'learning_rate': (0.01, 0.3)}
opt = BayesSearchCV(cat_model, param_space, n_iter=32, cv=3)
opt.fit(X, y)
print(f"ุฏูุช CatBoost: {opt.best_score_:.2%}")

# ุจุตุฑโุณุงุฒ
fig = go.Figure()
fig.add_trace(go.Candlestick(x=data_5min.index,
                             open=data_5min['Open'],
                             high=data_5min['High'],
                             low=data_5min['Low'],
                             close=data_5min['Close'], name='Price'))
fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=data_5min.index, y=data_5min['Quantum_Signal'], mode='lines', name='Quantum Signal'))
fig.update_layout(title='Quantum Cosmos: XAUUSD 5-Minute Chart - Inspired by Behrouz Bouzari',
                  xaxis_title='Time', yaxis_title='Price')
fig.show()

          (data_5min['Quantum_Signal'] > 0.6) & \
          ((data_5min['RSI'] < 30) | (data_5min['MACD'] > data_5min['MACD_Signal'])) & \
          (data_5min['Hour'].isin([8, 9, 10, 11, 13, 14, 15, 16]))
